The issue is:\n\n1. **Parsing**: CSS calc() expressions are parsed in `servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs`\n\n2. **Computing**: The computed values use `servo/components/style/values/computed/length_percentage.rs` which has `CalcLengthPercentage::resolve()` that calls `resolve_map()`\n\n3. **Resolution/Arithmetic**: The actual arithmetic happens in:\n   - `servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs` in `resolve_internal()` and the arithmetic operations\n   - `servo/components/style/values/computed/length_percentage.rs` in `CalcLengthPercentageLeaf` trait implementation\n\n4. **Overflow issue**: The arithmetic operations (addition, multiplication) in lines like:\n   - Line 815 in length_percentage.rs: `*one += *other;` (no overflow check)\n   - Line 838 in length_percentage.rs: `*left *= *right;` (no overflow check)\n   - Line 870 in length_percentage.rs: Result of `op(one.px(), other.px())` (no overflow check)\n 593-599 only handles the AllowedNumericType clamping, not overflow from extreme arithmetic operations.\n\n6. **C++ Integration**: `layout/style/ServoStyleConstsInlines.h` has the C++ bindings that call the Servo functions.\n\nSo the files are:\n- `servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs` (parsing)\n- `servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs` (calc node handling and This clamping happens AFTER overflow has already occurred:\\n\\n```rust\\nLength::new(self.clamping_mode.clamp(px.px())).normalized()  // Line 1004 in length_percentage.rs\\n```\\n\\nOnce a value has overflowed to infinity, `clamp()` cannot recover the original intent.\\n\\n## C++ Integration Points\\n\\nThe Servo Rust code integrates with C++ Firefox through:\\n\\n1. **FFI Gateway** (`servo/ports/geckolib/glue.rs`, line 9208):\\n   ```rust\\n   pub extern \\\"C\\\" fn Servo_ResolveCalcLengthPercentage(\\n       calc: &computed::length_percentage::CalcLengthPercentage,\\n       basis: f32,\\n   ) -> f32 {\\n       calc.resolve(computed::Length::new(basis)).px()  // Calls resolve() which can overflow\\n   }\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **C++ Resolution** (`layout/style/ServoStyleConstsInlines.h`, lines 726-735):\\n   ```cpp\\n   CSSCoord StyleCalcLengthPercentage::ResolveToCSSPixels(CSSCoord aBasis) const {\\n       return Servo_ResolveCalcLengthPercentage(this, aBasis);  // Calls unprotected Rust resolution\\n   }\\n   ```\\n\\n## Summary of Vulnerable Files\\n\\n**Parsing**: `servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs` - parses CSS calc() syntax\\n\\n**Calc Tree Structure**: `servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs` - defines expression AST and resolution logic\\n\\n**Numeric Computation & Overflow**: `servo/components/style/values/computed/length_percentage.rs` - contains unprotected arithmetic operations (try_sum_in_place, try_product_in_place, try_op, map)\\n\\n**Clamping**: `servo/components/style_traits/values.rs` - provides post-computation clamping that cannot fix pre-existing overflow\\n\\n**FFI Bridge**: `servo/ports/geckolib/glue.rs` - Servo_ResolveCalcLengthPercentage function that calls vulnerable Rust code\\n\\n**C++ Integration**: `layout/style/ServoStyleConstsInlines.h` - StyleCalcLengthPercentage::Resolve methods that invoke the FFI\\n\\nThe crash occurs because extreme calc() values overflow during intermediate arithmetic operations, producing infinity or NaN, which then cause issues downstream in Firefox's layout or rendering pipeline.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
